  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_c81f10a2-3073-4329-9976-df561e7d5982'
      });
    }

      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"

<span id="freeTextContainer11920449270454410174"><i>Step into the world of Shadow Falls, a camp that helps teens tap into their special... talents.   <span id="freeText11920449270454410174" style="display:none"><i>Step into the world of Shadow Falls, a camp that helps teens tap into their special... talents. Once you visit, you’ll never forget it—and you’ll never, ever be the same.</i><br /><br />From the moment Kylie Galen arrived at Shadow Falls Camp, she’s had one burning question: What am I? Surrounded by vampires, werewolves, shape-shifters, fairies and witches, Kylie longs to figure out her own supernatural identity…and what her burgeoning powers mean. And now she’ll need them more than ever, because she’s being haunted by a new spirit who insists that someone Kylie knows—and loves—will die before the end of the summer. If only she only knew who she was supposed to save. And how...<br /><br />But giving Kylie the most trouble is her aching heart. Gorgeous werewolf Lucas left camp with another girl, but he’s still visiting Kylie in her dreams. And Derek, a sexy half Fae who’s always been there for her when she needed him, is pushing to get more serious—and growing impatient, especially when Lucas returns. Kylie knows she needs to decide between the boys, and it’s tearing her up inside. <br /><br />Yet romance will have to wait, because something from the dark side of the supernatural world is hiding in Shadow Falls. It’s about to threaten everything she holds dear... and bring her closer to her destiny.</span>

  <div class="friendReviews elementListBrown" >
    <div class="section firstReview">
      

<div id="review_158758951" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/158758951" />
    <a title="Mateja" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2655289-mateja"><img alt="Mateja" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1546419254p2/2655289.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/158758951?book_show_action=true">Apr 04, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mateja" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mateja" href="/user/show/2655289-mateja">Mateja</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer158758951" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13915651063343772592">C.C. Hunter wrote an amazing sequel to Born at Midnight. Everything I loved about Born at Midnight was present in Awake at Dawn. Awake at Dawn is absolutely unputdownable. I read this book in record time. I got up an hour early in the morning to read, I read on the bus on my way to class, I even ignored my friends at break time in order to immerse myself in Kylie's story. <br/><br/>Awake at dawn is a delightful read with a plot full of twists and turns, genuine emotions that reach your heart and make you </span>
  <span id="freeText13915651063343772592" style="display:none">C.C. Hunter wrote an amazing sequel to Born at Midnight. Everything I loved about Born at Midnight was present in Awake at Dawn. Awake at Dawn is absolutely unputdownable. I read this book in record time. I got up an hour early in the morning to read, I read on the bus on my way to class, I even ignored my friends at break time in order to immerse myself in Kylie's story. <br /><br />Awake at dawn is a delightful read with a plot full of twists and turns, genuine emotions that reach your heart and make you helpless against loving the characters. Every character in this series is just so alive, their personalities are so strong, it feels like you're reading about your own friends and enemies. No character is unnecessary, each and every one of them plays a major role in Kylie's life (positive and negative). <br /><br />Kylie's friends, Miranda and Della, with their clashing personalities, their kindness and devotion to Kylie provide the book with many delightful moments, and gut wrenching ones too. And Holiday along with Burnett is such a positive role model for all the kids at camp. The relationship between the two camp leaders (business and personal) adds to the richness of the book. Kylie's relationship with Holiday was especially heart warming. Holiday filled the role of a supportive big sister perfectly. <br /><br />Kylie herself is a wonderful main character, with kindness that she offers even to those who in my opinion don't deserve it. All her emotions and reactions are so genuine and realistic I found myself crying when she did, laughing when she did. She's a wonderful example of a teen trying to find herself and to define her role in this world. She’s long from figuring all that out, but despite all the hurdles that are thrown in her way she stays true to herself, even in the most difficult situations. <br /><br />Now, what to say about the boys...Oh, the boys. I have to admit I was leaning heavily toward Derek in this book and rooted for him. For once I wanted the kind and loving character, who is always there for the girl, to in the end win her over. And just as I was set on wanting Derek and Kylie together, C.C. Hunter added Lucas and his charmingly honest personality to the mix, leaving me yet again undecided about the love issue.<br /><br />Without a doubt, Awake at Dawn is worth buying, reading and displaying it on your bookshelf. The third book (and hopefully not the final book), Taken at Dusk is one of my most anticipated books in the year of 2012.</span>
  <a data-text-id="13915651063343772592" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <a title="Jen ♥Star-Crossed Book Blog♥" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jen ♥Star-Crossed Book Blog♥" href="/user/show/28353412-jen-star-crossed-book-blog">Jen ♥Star-Crossed Book Blog♥</a>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28353412-jen-star-crossed-book-blog?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28353412-jen-star-crossed-book-blog?shelf=creatures-vampire">creatures-vampire</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2335720473" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8127004677553251161">Well, <b>I won't be continuing this series. The issues I had with the first book, became even more glaring in Awake at Dawn.</b> My main two issues were -<br/><br/>✮ <b>The pace seemed to drag even more. </b> <br/><blockquote>
  "....I mean, if I understand this right, someone is going to die. Actually die and it’s not going to be an easy death, either.” All the problems in Kylie’s life started bouncing around her head like ping-pong balls. Tears filled her eyes. It still hurt to think about her grandmother’s funeral—she couldn’t lose </blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText8127004677553251161" style="display:none">Well, <b>I won't be continuing this series. The issues I had with the first book, became even more glaring in Awake at Dawn.</b> My main two issues were -<br><br>✮ <b>The pace seemed to drag even more. </b> <br><blockquote>
  "....I mean, if I understand this right, someone is going to die. Actually die and it’s not going to be an easy death, either.” All the problems in Kylie’s life started bouncing around her head like ping-pong balls. Tears filled her eyes. It still hurt to think about her grandmother’s funeral—she couldn’t lose someone else. “Failure isn’t an option.”
</blockquote><br>I continually felt as though I kept getting pulled out of the story. It didn't seem to hold my interest, and when I would put the book down, I didn't have the urge to pick it back up. On top of that, <b>I wasn't the biggest fan for how the storyline proceeded.</b> It wasn't a path that held by interest, which made me feel so sad.<br><br>✮ <b>I'm not happy with the love triangle.</b> <br><blockquote>
  He leaned closer. “I’m patient, Kylie. I’ve waited eleven years for you. I can wait until you’re ready.”
</blockquote><br>Again, it's being dragged out. Just like the pace. So by the end of the book, there was definitely a clear winner. Or I guess it would be better to say that Kylie had more of a connection to one of the guys than the other. Which made me ecstatic, yet Kylie put it all on pause. It was not moving forward, even by that last page, and it left me feeling irritated. I'm not a fan of love triangles being stretched out, and this one definitely was.<br><br>I usually don't stop in the middle of a series, I can be a little neurotic and need to know how it all ends. Even if I'm not a huge fan. But I went and sneaked a peak at the next few books, to make for sure that I was making the correct decision. And what I saw <i>definitely</i> solidified my reason to stop this series now. All my issues kept appearing in the next few books. So I'm done and walking away. <b>While I'm sure there are plenty of people who will love or have loved this series, unfortunately I just can't be one of them.</b><br><br><i>For more of my reviews, please visit:</i> <br><a title="Star-Crossed Book Blog" href="http://starcrossedbookblog.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_234951773" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/234951773" />
    <a title="Beatriz  Lins" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4614263-beatriz-lins"><img alt="Beatriz  Lins" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1577975892p2/4614263.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/234951773?book_show_action=true">Nov 13, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Beatriz  Lins" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Beatriz  Lins" href="/user/show/4614263-beatriz-lins">Beatriz  Lins</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer234951773" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10458929594382518972">Born at Midnight was a great start to this series. I liked the writing, and even though Kylie was boring sometimes, it was still enjoyable. I didn't like certain things about it, like the shallow romance, and the mistery about what Kylie was. <br/>I hoped that, in Awake at Dawn, those things would develop, and we'd get to know a lot more about Shadow Falls. I can say, for sure, that this didn't happen. <br/>Well, to start with, Kylie doesn't know what she is. She spends the first half of the book searchin</span>
  <span id="freeText10458929594382518972" style="display:none">Born at Midnight was a great start to this series. I liked the writing, and even though Kylie was boring sometimes, it was still enjoyable. I didn't like certain things about it, like the shallow romance, and the mistery about what Kylie was. <br />I hoped that, in Awake at Dawn, those things would develop, and we'd get to know a lot more about Shadow Falls. I can say, for sure, that this didn't happen. <br />Well, to start with, Kylie doesn't know what she is. She spends the first half of the book searching for answers, and when she doesn't get them, she starts to look for her grandparents. And big surprise, this research leads us nowhere. I get it that the autor wants a suspense, but it's boring. I can't stand another internal crisis, with Kylie wondering what she is, and being completely broken by it. Seriously, get a grip. Strong female characters are one of the things that attract me in a book,and someone who just complains about the lack of answers and does little about it isn't appealing. <br />The romance is also disappointing. Kylie likes Derek, but can't give her heart to him because she still thinks about Lucas (the shape-shifter who left the camp for unknown reasons). And, of course, when Lucas comes back, her whole frame shakes and her pulse speeds up at the sight of him, while at the same time, she tries to fall in love with Derek. Love triangles are great, as long as they are well-written. And this one wasn't. It was a mess of feelings and impulses, and I still don't understand Kylie's preferences. <br />Lucas, apparently, is supposed to be charming, and a badboy. I got the impression he's a jerk covered with sweet words. He leaves the girl, knowing that she may have feelings for another man, comes back later and expects to find her waiting for him. And when she hesitates, he tries to win her by making her remember how their love is amazing. <br />Oh, and did I mention that while he was gone, Kylie dreamed about them making out? And that the dreams aren't just a fragment of her imagination, but a psychic ability?<br />Not to mention that every 20 pages or so, Kylie talked to Holiday about every single thing that happened with her. Yes, she wanted to have a friend and yes, it's great to have heart-to-heart conversations, but with the camp leader? I know I wouldn't open up and spill all my problems in front of the principal of my school, no matter how many times she tells me I'm her friend. <br />Another disappointment was Miranda and Della. Yes, Della being a vampire and Miranda being a witch really makes their friendship that much harder, but the constant fight between the two of them was really childish. There wasn't even an argument, just constant insults. My point is, wanna make a troubled friendship? Fine. But make it believable. <br />One of the things I liked about Awake at Dawn, though, was Kylie's relationship with her mother. The way they cared about each other was great, and there was a specific part of the book that I really enjoyed. However, while their love was great, the change of personality in her mother was obvious. It could have been more subtle. <br />I really hate to write negative reviews. I do. But my mind was going to explode in frustration when I finished this book. I know others may have loved it, but it was ... not so good for me. I'm still going to read Taked at Dusk, though. I'm hoping it'll get better. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="10458929594382518972" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_215778055" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/215778055" />
    <a title="Amber I." class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3632431-amber-i"><img alt="Amber I." src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1432490474p2/3632431.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/215778055?book_show_action=true">Sep 26, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Amber I." class="user" itemprop="url" name="Amber I." href="/user/show/3632431-amber-i">Amber I.</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer215778055" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12876179357460533699">I would like to just say I NEED MORE LUCAS! Okay so you might guess I am a total hot werewolf fan. While I loved every minute he was in this book, I would like more, lots and lots more!!<br/><br/>Awake at Dawn is a fantastic sequel. All of our favorites are back and just as loveable as before. Its just a fun new series with an amazing set of characters, one hot werewolf (okay the fairy is too, lol) and lots of mystery. Kylie is still trying to figure out what supernatural she really is. Now she is gaining</span>
  <span id="freeText12876179357460533699" style="display:none">I would like to just say I NEED MORE LUCAS! Okay so you might guess I am a total hot werewolf fan. While I loved every minute he was in this book, I would like more, lots and lots more!!<br /><br />Awake at Dawn is a fantastic sequel. All of our favorites are back and just as loveable as before. Its just a fun new series with an amazing set of characters, one hot werewolf (okay the fairy is too, lol) and lots of mystery. Kylie is still trying to figure out what supernatural she really is. Now she is gaining all these new talents and turning into one bad ass supernatural (whatever that might be) but nothing is clear, is she a werewolf, vampire, shape-shifter or something completely different? <br /><br /><br />I must say Awake at Dawn is addicting. Somewhere close to the middle, I knew I had to finish that day or I would not be able to sleep. I needed my answers and I just knew if I waited a little longer I would get some Lucas action. C.C Hunter really brings these characters to life and you feel like you know them. You have her two best friends: a take no crap vampire Della, and a little not to sure of herself witch Miranda, both are always there and you feel such a connection. Then there is her two boys, sensitive and loveable fairy Derek, then hot and mysterious Lucas who will have you totally teaming them up. Not to mention Holiday, Perry her mom and the ghosts who play important rolls. <br /><br /><br /><br />Lets just say if you like a fun supernatural read with an awesome set of characters and a story that keeps you guessing, well you are going to love Awake at Dawn!</span>
  <a data-text-id="12876179357460533699" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1743644511" />

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Hardcover " href="/book/show/16172466-trezita-in-zori-de-zi">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/58427946-dana-cristiana?shelf=hardcover">hardcover</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/58427946-dana-cristiana?shelf=the-big-mystery">the-big-mystery</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/58427946-dana-cristiana?shelf=from-the-library">from-the-library</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/58427946-dana-cristiana?shelf=fantasy-books">fantasy-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/58427946-dana-cristiana?shelf=teenager-life">teenager-life</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1743644511" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5598860220755362678">3,5 stars / 5.<br/><br/>This sequel was far more interesting than the first "Shadow Falls" novel; especially in the beginning. But in the middle it was just a long process where little concrete things were happening.<br/>Kylie Galen met another ghost now, a woman. One that kept telling Kylie that someone dear to her will die soon and that she has to save that person. But Kylie didn't knew exactly who she refers to.<br/><br/>Kylie goes to the waterfall, but no big deal is happening. She is trying to find her grandparents</span>
  <span id="freeText5598860220755362678" style="display:none">3,5 stars / 5.<br /><br />This sequel was far more interesting than the first "Shadow Falls" novel; especially in the beginning. But in the middle it was just a long process where little concrete things were happening.<br />Kylie Galen met another ghost now, a woman. One that kept telling Kylie that someone dear to her will die soon and that she has to save that person. But Kylie didn't knew exactly who she refers to.<br /><br />Kylie goes to the waterfall, but no big deal is happening. She is trying to find her grandparents; to see what supernatural creatures they are. Because not even in the sequel we aren't going to find out what is she. At the end, though, we can imagine. We can see her throughout the novel growing; her body, at least. She even grows stronger.<br /><br />But anyway... again, you need to be very patient with the novel and certain parts of it, because it goes slowly. The story itself is a very interesting one; it kept me curious. It's just that it is very slow and the revealing moments aren't all that good or "wow". But overall, it was a good read, and let me tell you, that ending...<br /><br />There were things that I didn't fully understood, but they don't affect me liking the book too much. It had much more mystery than the first one as far as I can remember, so enjoy this.<br /><br />*Sorry for my repetitive review. I am really tired right now.*</span>

<div id="review_185277081" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/185277081" />
    <a title="Danny" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3254909-danny"><img alt="Danny" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1301556302p2/3254909.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/185277081?book_show_action=true">Jul 15, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Danny" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Danny" href="/user/show/3254909-danny">Danny</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9781429984997" href="/book/show/11522182-awake-at-dawn">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3254909-danny?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3254909-danny?shelf=july2-imm">july2-imm</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer185277081" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5766957348593419660">Saying I was thrilled when Awake at Dawn arrived on my doorstep would out it lightly. I was beyond thrilled because after finishing Born At Midnight I was in love with the story, the characters and CC's writing. I devoured Awake at Dawn in one day and needless to day I was sad when it was over... <br/><br/>We are back in Shadow Falls with Kylie, her great friends, the boys and the camp leaders. Kylie still has no clue who she is and what she will become other than knowing and finally accepting her ghost-w</span>
  <span id="freeText5766957348593419660" style="display:none">Saying I was thrilled when Awake at Dawn arrived on my doorstep would out it lightly. I was beyond thrilled because after finishing Born At Midnight I was in love with the story, the characters and CC's writing. I devoured Awake at Dawn in one day and needless to day I was sad when it was over... <br /><br />We are back in Shadow Falls with Kylie, her great friends, the boys and the camp leaders. Kylie still has no clue who she is and what she will become other than knowing and finally accepting her ghost-whispering gift.<br />But she is still confused and desperately wants to know who and what she is. <br />With Lucas gone, she's drawn even closer to Derek who never hided his deep affection for Kylie. But other Love stories and romances unfold during the story. There is Miranda and her crush on Perry the powerful shape shifter and there is Holiday the camp leader and the Vampire... <br /><br />In Awake at Dawn friendships and relationships, that have been formed in Born At Midnight grow deeper and more meaningful and I loved seeing this. The unusal friendship between Della, Miranda and Kylie is beautiful. The girls fight and piss themselves off ever so often but in the end they love each other and are truly loyal. <br /><br />Kylie grows and comes slowly to terms with being supernatural and not "normal" anymore. Still, deep down she's lonely since she still is no step further about discovering her true self. But in Awake at Dawn we will see Kylie grow even more exceptional than she already is and there are a few twists and turns you might not expect that were truly intriguing. <br /><br />Kylie and the boys... Oh My.. the boys! Lucas is gone and Derek is there trying to get Kylie's full attention, but she's still reluctant to fully commit to Derek. She stands herself in the way of letting her emotions loose, but on the other side there is still Lucas in her mind... <br /><br />I admit, I fell for Lucas in Born At Midnight but now I am so very torn. Derek really really grew in this book and I crushed hard on him here... He's sexy, hot, sweet, cute and ..did I say hot? I remember CC saying that people who are Team Lucas might change their mind after reading Awake at Dawn... well she didn't promise too much. I still love Lucas (a lot!!) but now, I'm torn between those two hot boys, just like Kylie... <br /><br />I also very much love the deep connection she has with Holiday the Camp leader. They are more than just "teacher" and "student" she's more than a sister and I loved that Kylie had someone she could confide to ... <br /><br />Awake at Dawn was full of growing relationships, friendships, love and romance. Following Kylie's journey to discover her true self was wonderful and I loved every minute I spend with Kylie and the others. This will be a series that will have a place in my heart with characters I deeply care for and love. I can't wait to learn more about Kylie, I can't wait to see who she will choose and I can't wait to hear more about Holiday, Miranda, Perry and Della.. Is there a place for me in the Shadow Falls camp? ...</span>
  <a data-text-id="5766957348593419660" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14811808-liz?shelf=magical-creatures">magical-creatures</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer510179868" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10717641675727512045"><blockquote>
  <b>“Life isn't supposed to be easy. Generally speaking, the harder something is the more rewarding the results will be.”</b>
</blockquote><br/><blockquote>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380405723i/790832.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</blockquote><br/><i>This is one of series that seem to get better with each book. I am glad I decided to read this one.</i><br/><br/>In this book a new ghost starts to visit Kylie and warns her that someone she loves will die soon, but Kylie does not understand whom she has to save. <br/>Moreover, there is the problem with vampire attacks and her supernatural identity. The hints are all contradictory and Kylie </span>
  <span id="freeText10717641675727512045" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <b>“Life isn't supposed to be easy. Generally speaking, the harder something is the more rewarding the results will be.”</b>
</blockquote><br><blockquote>
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380405723i/790832.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</blockquote><br><i>This is one of series that seem to get better with each book. I am glad I decided to read this one.</i><br><br>In this book a new ghost starts to visit Kylie and warns her that someone she loves will die soon, but Kylie does not understand whom she has to save. <br>Moreover, there is the problem with vampire attacks and her supernatural identity. The hints are all contradictory and Kylie is more and more confused. The boy-problem seems rather harmless in comparison with the ghost and the vampire attacks, but all of these problems really bother Kylie. <br><blockquote>
  <b>“What you are doesn't matter. Because what you are isn't going to change who you are.”</b>
</blockquote><br>Kylie is a very sympathetic character. She is like an angel of peace, who helps Holiday and Della and Miranda with their problems and does not bother anyone with her own worries. <br>Kylie is determined and very humorous and I really like her in this book, while I did not like her in the first book. <br>Della and Miranda are both loyal and hilarious persons. They are worth Kylie, together they are a real dream-team when Miranda and Della don't fight. <br>I don't really like Derek, he seems to perfect and too soft to me. Besides, his words and actions are often contradictory. A point in favor of him is that he accepts Kylie no matter who she is and how she is, he just wants her to be honest and sure about her feelings. <br>Lucas is absent most of the time but when he appears he is very confident and caring and possessive. He is more of a real man in contrast to Derek. <br><blockquote>
  <b>“When we care about people, we sometimes overstep our grounds.”</b>
</blockquote><br>I honestly do like this book much more than the first one thanks to all the surprises and turning points and contradictory hints and feelings the characters have. <br><br>Now after reading this one I am totally looking forward to read the next books!<br>This book is perfect for all the House of Night fans, and those who love YA-fantasy series. </span>

          </span>

<div id="review_2512731782" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2512731782" />
    <a title="Caitlin Smith" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/50994603-caitlin-smith"><img alt="Caitlin Smith" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1551366765p2/50994603.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2512731782?book_show_action=true">Aug 30, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Caitlin Smith" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Caitlin Smith" href="/user/show/50994603-caitlin-smith">Caitlin Smith</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2512731782" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7569363702086675249">This series is so fun and entertaining!<br/><br/>Awake at Dawn continues on from Born at Midnight and Kylie has finally come to terms with her situation. As new abilities awaken within Kylie, she longs to find an answer whilst also being haunted by a spirit that insists someone Kylie loves is going to die unless she stops it. Caught between a half fae with a kind heart and a mysterious werewolf she shares a past with, Kylie must figure out what is going on and who she chooses. <br/><br/>Kylie was such a better char</span>
  <span id="freeText7569363702086675249" style="display:none">This series is so fun and entertaining!<br /><br />Awake at Dawn continues on from Born at Midnight and Kylie has finally come to terms with her situation. As new abilities awaken within Kylie, she longs to find an answer whilst also being haunted by a spirit that insists someone Kylie loves is going to die unless she stops it. Caught between a half fae with a kind heart and a mysterious werewolf she shares a past with, Kylie must figure out what is going on and who she chooses. <br /><br />Kylie was such a better character in this book compared to the first! She felt a lot more matured and a lot less judgemental. She’s a very determined, strong and protective character that I feel was portrayed very realistically. I really liked the development of her relationship with her mother. In the first book her mother was portrayed as not the best mother, but I loved seeing the two build this new and enjoyable relationship. I also really enjoyed the moments with Kylie and Daniel, her biological father, and when Kylie was struggling or in a difficult situation she looked for the support of her father’s ghost. Kylie developed quite a few new powers and abilities in this book and I loved seeing her wholeheartedly accept that she is supernatural in some way. <br /><br />One of my favourite things about this series is the relationship between Kylie, Della and Miranda. They all have such different personalities but they are so loyal to one another. I really loved when Miranda trapped Tabitha, a witch, in a cage. It was so funny! Also, I feel like we have seen a fair bit more of depth to Della’s character and I really like that! <br /><br />I love Holiday’s character. She is the authority figure you want in your life! She didn’t read quite as teen like as she did in the first book, which was good. I absolutely love the sisterly relationship she and Kylie have, it’s so lovely and enjoyable. Also I can’t wait to see what happens between Holiday and Burnett!<br /><br />Derek vs. Lucas. Derek is sweet, patient and caring however I just don’t care! I find Derek to be quite annoying and rather stupid to be honest, he wanted Kylie to be with him and just as she was going to tell him she wanted that to, he changed his mind! What?!?! I really like Lucas. From the beginning, I’ve enjoyed Lucas’s character more than Derek’s. I found him to be a lot more interesting and I think there’s more chemistry between Kylie and Lucas. <br /><br />I have to say, I did not see the Sara plot line coming! I won’t go into detail, but I thought the way it was put into the story worked really well. A big question in this book is, what supernatural is Kylie? We still don’t know! I kind of expected to find out by now but we still haven’t... <br /><br />Overall, this was a enjoyable read. While it’s definitely not the best in terms of writing and storyline, it’s a fun and easy book to read!</span>
  <a data-text-id="7569363702086675249" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_345786253" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/345786253" />
    <a title="Emily" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2917914-emily"><img alt="Emily" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/f_50x66-6a03a5c12233c941481992b82eea8d23.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/345786253?book_show_action=true">Jun 10, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Emily" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Emily" href="/user/show/2917914-emily">Emily</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2917914-emily?shelf=advisory-2011-2012">advisory-2011-2012</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
                  <em>
                    This review has been hidden because it contains spoilers. To view it,
                    <a href="#" onclick="Effect.toggle(&#39;reviewTextContainer345786253&#39;); return false;">click here.</a>
                  </em>
              <span id="reviewTextContainer345786253" class="readable"
                    style="display:none"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11591759714211333715"> After reading the first book in the series, Born at Midnight, I just had to read the second book because of the cliff hanger that was presented. Awake at Dawn was a mystical book that once again brought me back to shadow falls, a camp full of supernatural creatures. The protagonist Kylie Galen still isn’t able to figure out what type of supernatural creature she is and she is determined to find out. Although she might just look like a teenage girl on the outside the power she holds within her i</span>
  <span id="freeText11591759714211333715" style="display:none"> After reading the first book in the series, Born at Midnight, I just had to read the second book because of the cliff hanger that was presented. Awake at Dawn was a mystical book that once again brought me back to shadow falls, a camp full of supernatural creatures. The protagonist Kylie Galen still isn’t able to figure out what type of supernatural creature she is and she is determined to find out. Although she might just look like a teenage girl on the outside the power she holds within her is far stronger than anyone in the camp. Throughout the book the reader is exposed to more of Kylie’s powers. It seems as though her power matures along with her. At the beginning of the camp she is confused and doesn’t understand the supernatural creatures that exist in the world. Although she is one, she was isolated from the rest. But as time passes in the camp, she realizes their existence and hers. I feel like because she was able to accept who she is her powers began to show more frequently. She goes on different searches to figure out what lies within her. With each path she takes a new truth is opened to her. Helping ghost is just a mere part of her powers. She can dreamscape and when she thought that the werewolf counselor had done harm to her mother, the strength of her power is shown as she was able to take down a werewolf. Same goes when Lucas (her werewolf crush) was locked up by rogue vampires when coming to save her, she broke down a concrete wall to save him. Confused about her powers and told she was a protector (one who has the powers to protect others but not herself) she searches for her biological grandparents from her dad’s side (she doesn’t know them) to give her some answers.<br /><br /> Kylie is a fascinating character with great potential. She is someone you can depend on but sometimes I feel as if she makes the wrong decisions. She is so determined to find out who she really is she is oblivious to what is in front of her. She pushes aside her friends and her potential boyfriend(s) and takes the dangerous road that might not even have the answers. I really like her character, strong and protective, but I think she needs to just be a teenage girl and worry less about her powers and more about her life with friends and family. Miranda and Della are very caring friends, although they want to rip each other’s head off, they are always there for Kylie and I think it is time for Kylie to spend more time with them instead of figuring out the unknown. The answers will arrive sooner or later and she just needs to be patient. Overall i don't really see her character change from the first book because she is still confused as ever. Although she accepted being different, she doesn't know "what" she is or who to choose as her boyfriend! :)<br /><br /> Additionally this book incorporates romance as well. Should Kylie pick a half fae or a werewolf? I think she should pick Lucas the werewolf. Derek is sweet and kind but Lucas is all she thinks about. Lucas is the one she meet when she was little, the one who protected her, the one who will risk changing his bloodline just to love her. It bothers me that she cannot choose one or the other when it is obvious who she really likes. This book basically has everything a fantasy reader would want. The supernatural, the romance, the action and the mystery so I would recommend this book – IT IS AWESOME. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="11591759714211333715" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_317407141" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/317407141" />
    <a title="J. Lee" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5250082-j-lee"><img alt="J. Lee" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1357341439p2/5250082.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/317407141?book_show_action=true">Apr 23, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="J. Lee" class="user" itemprop="url" name="J. Lee" href="/user/show/5250082-j-lee">J. Lee</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer317407141" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16653164942429112815">Kylie doesn’t know what she is. Kylie kisses a boy. Kylie has a sudden not-so-climatic event. Kylie still doesn’t what she is. Kylie is at the end of book two. <br/>For me, that was exactly what it was like reading this book. I remember I complained about the fact that Hunter didn’t use first person in the first installment of this series and unfortunately I have to do it again. In my opinion, if you’re going to write in third person, you should write in a way that your characters name isn’t repeated</span>
  <span id="freeText16653164942429112815" style="display:none">Kylie doesn’t know what she is. Kylie kisses a boy. Kylie has a sudden not-so-climatic event. Kylie still doesn’t what she is. Kylie is at the end of book two. <br />For me, that was exactly what it was like reading this book. I remember I complained about the fact that Hunter didn’t use first person in the first installment of this series and unfortunately I have to do it again. In my opinion, if you’re going to write in third person, you should write in a way that your characters name isn’t repeated in almost every sentence because it’s very distracting and highly annoying especially when you’ve chosen to give your character a name like Kylie (not that Kylie is a horrible name but say it over and over and over again and you’ll never want to hear it again). Also, I am definitely NOT a genius when it comes to grammar but I’m pretty sure that I came across several editing issues because they made my brain stutter and I had to go back and reread to make sure that there really was a word missing or misspelled and I hadn’t completely lost my mind. There were also a few times that Hunter added words into Kylie’s vocabulary or made her say things in a way that I don’t think matched her usual voice or style. For example, once she made her think, Gawd, to herself. For one, no one say GAWD! Not even us southern folks and certainly not Kylie.<br />I’m not saying this story was horrible. I’m sure a teenaged girl would love all the supernatural characters and reading about their different abilities and such, I did. However, it seemed to drone on and on about things that after a while I didn’t find so interesting because it was basically the same things that the first book droned on and on about. Kylie doesn’t know what she is. Ok. I get it. She wants desperately to find out. OK. Let’s do that. And she does but it’s only a little bit here and there without really doing anything significant or intriguing. And do we have to play out the entire conversation about the exact same thing that she has with Holiday in every single chapter? I also thought the character took it a little too far with, “I can’t kiss Derek because I don’t know what I am, I can’t not kiss Derek because I don’t know what I am, I can’t make up my mind between Derek and Lucas because I don’t know what I am….” <br />Ok, NEXT! I thought the idea behind the bloody ghost that kept visiting her played out pretty well. I was actually expecting something a little different. The surprise was taken away with all the extras the closer it got to the reveal but I guess it was necessary. As for the not-so-climatic event I mentioned earlier… I really don’t know what else to say about it. There were no surprises, no twists, no turns. It was pretty cut and dry.<br />I wouldn’t tell people not to read this series because there are some things that are interesting, just not intriguing. I am curious to find out what Kylie is, although right now it feels like Hunter is making up a character that isn’t realistic not even in this paranormal world because of her little-bit-of-everything status. As if she’s some freaky hybrid or something. We don’t drop our characters in vats of toxic wastes anymore…. So, why make them a hybrid, nonrealistic anomaly? <br /><br />P.S. I LOVE Della!<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="16653164942429112815" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2101652126" />
    <a title="Kathryn Ford" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7081484-kathryn-ford"><img alt="Kathryn Ford" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1575710913p2/7081484.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2101652126" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17244748975341365209">I give this book a solid 4 [yes I've been watching too many cooking competitions lately] I enjoyed this book just like I did the first one. I believe all teenagers should read this series because it deals with a lot of teen stuff and gives very wise advice. I also like the emphasis it places on friends and family. I guessed who was to be saved from the very beginning I just didn't know from what, so that part was slightly boring. But, the kick ass part of the book was good. </span>

Most of the time, she still has a ghost issue. She's figuring it all out and it's extremely interesting. I love her getting closer with Miranda and Della.   <span id="freeText1497556230984136152" style="display:none">The Good: Kylie still doesn't know what she is, so that still annoys the hell out of me. But, she's getting there. She's dealt. She's accepted. Most of the time, she still has a ghost issue. She's figuring it all out and it's extremely interesting. I love her getting closer with Miranda and Della. They have a very authentic teen girls at camp getting becoming friends thing going on, with all the insecurity and vulnerability that goes with that. Add in the varied types of paranormal they are and they're different personalities and it makes for some great interactions.I had my suspicions about what was going on so I wasn't completely shocked, but it was a great experience regardless.<br /><br />The Bad: At this point, the love triangle is unnecessary. Maybe it becomes important down the line, but right now it seems as though it's just one more thing distracting Kylie from figuring out what she is and what that means for her. </span>

I'm not telling her to throw herself at them either, but she holds back too much (which explain the Derek situatio</span>
  <span id="freeText6510058164788534046" style="display:none">This second book was totally better than the first one (even though I missed Lucas during half of the book). I think that there is a little character growth going on with Kylie which is a major improvement. She accepted that she's a supernatural and tries to know who she really is so she's on the right path. <br /><br />One thing I didn't like is how she always holds herself back with the boys. I'm not telling her to throw herself at them either, but she holds back too much (which explain the Derek situation at the end). She should either stop altogether talking to them or stop imagining things she doesn't want to happen or want to happen. If you really want something, go for it. So yeah, I didn't like the fact that she was really confused.<br /><br />I loved the mother-daughter situation. The two of them finally started to bond and it's just wonderful!!<br /><br />Overall, this book was really entertaining and I look forward to read the next book in the series!<br /><br />Also, omg spoilers: I so ship Holiday and Brunett</span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('JSb07sluNjTiJYMdxt+8R9b5U9vGdaU5hwAKos5BSlntt8KgdNDcGcLFO0g8swwiyByCYultS0WC6rI5cbMWtg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('zqZEjiDY99S4NZHoUc1yANP2dwSLVgaQlru10C1eCGgGN3LAnWYd+ZjVKb2rocJlzROmvaRO6OyTUQ1LkqxUhw==')})
  }

<span id="freeTextContainer13420460684447381566">C. C. Hunter is the New York Times bestselling author of over thirty-five books, including her wildly popular Shadow Falls and Shadow Falls: After Dark series. In addition to winning numerous awards and rave reviews for her novels, C.C. is also a photojournalist, motivational speaker, and writing coach. In February 2018, Wednesday Books will publish her contemporary young adult and hardcover debut</span>
  <span id="freeText13420460684447381566" style="display:none">C. C. Hunter is the New York Times bestselling author of over thirty-five books, including her wildly popular Shadow Falls and Shadow Falls: After Dark series. In addition to winning numerous awards and rave reviews for her novels, C.C. is also a photojournalist, motivational speaker, and writing coach. In February 2018, Wednesday Books will publish her contemporary young adult and hardcover debut, This Heart of Mine. And the first book of her new paranormal young adult series, The Mortician's Daughter: One Foot in the Grave was released on October 31st 2017. C. C. currently resides in Texas with her husband, junkyard dog, Lady, and whatever wild creatures that meander out from woods surrounding home.<br /><br />C.C. Hunter is a pseudonym. Her real name is Christie Craig and she also writes humorous romantic suspense romance novels. <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.christie-craig.com">www.christie-craig.com</a><br /><br /><br />C.C. would love to hear from you. Because of deadlines, it may take her a day or so to get back with you, but she will reply. cc@cchunterbooks.com</span>
